I've been collecting bottles and cans for buyback for years now. Once I discovered AIM, I swore I'd never go to another buyback center again. Fast and honest workers, and I know I'm getting fair prices for all my glass, plastic and aluminum. They even take metals like copper for great prices and the workers are very knowledgeable on what's what. I recently found out they take car batteries and appliances like refrigerators. Basically AIM is the only place I trust anymore. Too many bad experiences at their competitors. At AIM, I know I'm a valued customer and I feel welcome every time I stop by. Easily a 5 star buyback center.<//Text>

<Rating>5</Rating><review>Though this review is biased as I am an employee at AIM, I felt the need to let the public know that we will treat you right here. Here at AIM, we are family owned and operated. We are certified by the state of California to operate our Recycling Center and frequently have visits from the weights and measures division to insure our scales are accurate. Everything is in view for customers to see that they are getting the right weight and price for their hard earned material. We take a variety of material such as ferrous, non-ferrous, and CRV materials. Though often times there are rules or laws that prohibit us from paying for certain materials right away such as copper or brass, we make sure that once the holding period is up, the customer is paid promptly.
Come to AIM if you want honest hardworkers who treat you right.< /review><Date>1481308635491< /Date><Gmap_id>0x80859d6068dd43e5:0x38827118fbf5cc1< /Gmap_id>< userid>

<Review>After RePlanet closed at Safeway Pinole, there really aren't any convenient recycling centers servicing the Pinole/Richmond/El Cerrito neighborhoods. I'm so happy to discover American Iron & Metals or AIM!

So how this place works -you places cans in one or more trash bins (provided), bottles in another, load the bins on a hand cart (provided), and head on over to the scale! They even have a vehicle scale if you're hauling a truck load of scrap metal! You just drive your vehicle up on it, no need to unload it-amazing!!!

Also, they're conveniently open on Saturdays, they let you leave caps on the bottles, and they work very quickly -what more could you ask for? Well, me personally, I'd ask for a trash can. That's one thing this place is missing. They ask you to take your trash with you, bummer! And maybe some hand sanitizer, yeah, that would be great! But otherwise, this place is easily 5-stars! A lot of people are frustrated because they've been inconvenienced by this place, I know I have too, but it's not the company's fault business hours are listed incorrectly on Yelp, it's actually Yelp's fault! I have corrections currently pending, I hope it gets updated!</Review>< rating>
4< /rating>

<text>I wanted to provide a better written review so I made sure I visited at least five times in the last four months. The quality of the food here is good. I'd say it's a notch above most Mexican restaurants in town. The service is always excellent. The staff is kind and friendly and the place is clean. So why 3 stars? It's my opinion that the cook(s) have a heavy hand on adding salt. I've sampled most of their popular dishes and all I felt were too salty, especially the carne asada. I'm sure others will disagree with me, adding that Mexican food is inherently salty. But I've lived in San Diego all my life. I've eaten at close to 1000 Mexican food places across the country; there is a line between adding sodium for flavor and have overdone things. The customer can always add salt but once it's made with the food, it's too late.</text><user_id>117312323745695739631<//user_id><user_name>R M< /user_name>< rate>

<Rate>5< /Rate><text>I dined here solo and had a great experience. The place is small and have limited indoor seating, but the table turnover is very quick.

I ordered karaage, takoyaki and the gojiramen with pork belly. The ramen was phenomenal. Once you get a bite of every thing, pork belly, egg, noodles and soup, you smile because of how good it tastes.

< Review>
Absolutely wonderful. I don't live close by. It is worth the trip to this restaurant. We had breakfast there. I had 2 eggs with hash browns and toast. I updated the picture to include toast.  There are different options. Like you don't have to have the hash browns or toast. You can get bisquits and gravy instead of the toast. There is also potatoes with red and green peppers and onions. It is called "country spuds".  My husband had the panrita. I think that is the name. It is a pancake with eggs, bacon. He had some hash browns in it. It is all inside of the pancake. It is all so good. I can't say enough good things about it. Go there hungry. You won't be disappointed. Very tasty. Large portions. They have all kinds of breakfast items. Good, reasonable prices. Good for families or by yourself. Breakfast is from 7am to 11:00am. Stephanie is very nice, friendly and helpful. Rock's Place is now Rock's. Rock's also has lunch and dinner. They have an absolutely wonderful pizza. Great sandwiches. There is a lot of really good food. Karaoke is on Thursdays. It starts about 5pm. Lots of fun. I enjoy it. If you don't go there, you'll be missing out. Rocks is really cute inside. Lots of parking. See ya there.</Review>

Been here a couple times decent prices and usually pretty good if you go during the day though evening time tends to be a bit busier.

I give it a 4-star because of the times I've gone the coin machine usually is out of stock. Usually they have an attendant who will fix the issue and we can resolve it but it's one of those places that I would suggest getting quarters ahead of time before coming in.

Another issue is often I find the machines kind of slow for washing... But this is sort of counteracted as the dryers are pretty good for the price one quarter is about 10 minutes of high to low heat.< /text>

<review>The spin cycle on my washer broke, so I went to wash blankets, towels, linen n the piles of clothes that I couldn't (or didn't want to)wash by hand.
